Antarapeyyāle
Katipucchāvāro

Kati āpattiyo kati āpattikkhandhā, kati vinītavatthuni, kati agāravā, kati gāravā, kati vinītavatthūni, kati vipattiyo, kati āpattisamuṭṭhānā, kati vivādamūlāni, kati anuvādamūlāni, kati sārāṇiyā dhammā, kati bhedakaravatthūni, kati adhikaraṇāni, kati samathā:
Pañca āpattiyo, pañca āpattikkhandhā, pañca vinītavatthūni, satta āpattiyo, satta āpattikkhandhā, satta vinīta vatthūni, cha agāravā, cha gāravā, cha vinītavatthūni, catasso vipattiyo, cha āpattisamuṭṭhānā, cha vivādamūlāni, cha anuvādamūlāni, cha sārāṇiyā dhammā, aṭṭhārasa bhedakaravatthūni, cattāri adhikaraṇāni, sattasamathā

1. Tattha katamā pañca āpattiyo: pārājikāpatti, saŋghādisesāpatti, pācittiyāpatti, pāṭidesanīyāpatti, dukkaṭāpatti. Imā pañca āpattitiyo

2. Kattha katame pañca āpattikkhandhā: pārājikāpattikkhandho, saŋghādisesāpattikkhandho, pācittiyāpattikkhandho, pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandho dukkaṭāpattikkhandho, ime pañca āpattikkhandhā

3. Tattha katamāni pañca vinītavatthūni: pañcahi āpattikkhandhehi ārati virati paṭivirati veramaṇi akiriyā akaraṇaɱ anajjhāpatti velāanatikkamo setughāto, imāni pañca vinītavatthūni.

4. Tattha katamā satta āpattiyo: pārājikāpatti, saŋghādisesāpatti, thullaccayāpatti, pācittiyāpatti, pāṭidesanīyāpatti, dukkaṭāpatti. Dubbhāsitāpatti. Imā satta āpattiyo

5. Tattha katame satta āpattikkhandhā: pārājikāpattikkhandho, saŋghādisesāpattikkhandho thullaccayāpattikkhandho, pācittiyāpattikkhandho, pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandho dukkaṭāpattikkhandho, ime satta āpattikkhandhā.
6. Tattha katamāni satta vinītavatthūni: sattahi āpattikkhandhehi ārati virati paṭivirati veramaṇi akiriyā akaraṇaɱ anajjhāpatti celāanatikkamo setughāto, imāni satta vinītavatthūni.

7. Tattha katame cha agāravā: buddhe agāravo, dhamme agāravo, saŋghe agāravo, sikkhāya agāravo, appamāde agāravo, paṭisanthāre agāravo. Ime cha agāravā.

[BJT Page 318]
[page 092]

8. Tattha katame cha gāravā: buddhe gāravo, dhamme gāravo, saŋghe gāravo, sikkhāya gāravo, appamāde gāravo, paṭisanthāre gāravo. Ime cha gāravā.
9. Tattha katamāni cha vinītavatthūni: chahi agāravehi, ārati virati paṭivirati veramaṇi akiriyā akaraṇaɱ anajjhāpatti velāanatikkamo setughāto imāni cha vinītavatthūni.
10. Tattha katamā catasso vipattiyo: sīlavipatti, ācāravipatti, diṭṭhivipatti, ājivavipatti imā catasso vipattiyo.

11. Tattha katame cha āpattisamuṭṭhānā: atthāpatti kāyato samuṭṭhāti, na vācato na cittato atthāpatti vācato samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato na cittato, atthāpatti kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhāti na cittato, atthāpatti kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato atthāpatati vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhati, na kāyato atthāpatti kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti. Ime cha āpattisamuṭṭhānā

12. Tattha katamāni cha vivādamūlāni: idha bhikkhū kodhano hoti upanāhī, yo so bhikkhū kodhano hoti upanāhi, so sattharipi agāravo viharati appatissavo, dhammepi agāravo viharati appatissavo, saŋghepi agāravo viharati appatissavo, sikkhāyapi na paripūrakāri hoti yo so bhikkhū satthari agāravo viharati appatissavo, dhamme agāravo viharati appatissavo, saŋghe agāravo viharati appatissavo, sikkhāya na paripūrakāri hoti yo so bhikkhu satthari agāravo viharati appatissavo, dhamme agāravo viharati appatissavo, saŋghe agāravo viharati appatissavo, sikkhāya na paripūrakāri hoti so saŋghe vivādaɱ janeti, yo hoti vivādo bahujanaahitāya bahujanaasubāya bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaɱ evarūpaɱ ce tumhe vivādamūlaɱ ajjhattaɱ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha, tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlassa pahānāya vāyameyyātha evarūpaɱ ce tumhe vivādamūlaɱ ajjhattaɱ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha, tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiɱ anavassavāya paṭipajjeyyātha evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa pahānaɱ hoti, evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiɱ anavassavo hoti

Punacaparaɱ bhikkhu makkhī hoti palāsī. Parāmāsī hoti ādhānagāhī duppaṭinissaggī,yo so bhikkhū sandiṭṭhiparāmāsī hoti ādhānagāhī duppaṭinissaggī, so sattharipi agāravo viharati appatissavo, dhammepi agāravo viharati appatissavo, saŋghepi agāravo viharati appatissavo, sikkhāyapi na paripūrakāri hoti yo so bhikkhū satthari agāravo viharati appatissavo, dhamme agāravo viharati appatissavo, saŋghe agāravo viharati appatissavo, sikkhāya na paripūrakāri hoti so saŋghe vivādaɱ janeti, yo hoti vivādo bahujanaahitāya bahujanaasubāya bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaɱ evarūpaɱ ce tumhe vivādamūlaɱ ajjhattaɱ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha, tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlakassa pahānāya vāyameyyātha evarūpaɱ ce tumhe vivādamūlaɱ ajjhattaɱ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha, tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiɱ anavassāvāya paṭipajjeyyātha evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa pahānaɱ hoti, evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiɱ anavassavo hoti

Punacaparaɱ bhikkhu issakī hoti maccharī sandiṭṭhi parāmāsī hoti ādhānagāhī duppaṭinissaggī, yo so bhikkhū sandiṭṭhi parāmāsī hoti ādhānagāhī duppaṭinissaggī so sattharipi agāravo viharati appatissavo, dhammepi agāravo viharati appatissavo, saŋghepi agāravo viharati appatissavo, sikkhāyapi na paripūrakāri hoti yo so bhikkhu satthari agāravo viharati appatissavo, dhamme agāravo viharati appatissavo, saŋghe agāravo viharati appatissavo, sikkhāya na paripūrakārī hoti so saŋghe vivādaɱ janeti, yo hoti vivādo bahujanaahitāya bahujanaasubāya bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaɱ evarūpaɱ ce tumhe vivādamūlaɱ ajjhattaɱ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha, tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlakassa pahānāya vāyameyyātha evarūpaɱ ce tumhe vivādamūlaɱ ajjhattaɱ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha, tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiɱ anavassavāya paṭipajjeyyātha evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa pahānaɱ hoti, evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiɱ anavassavo hoti

Punacaparaɱ bhikkhū saṭho hoti māyāvī sandiṭṭhi parāmāsī hoti ādhānagāhī duppaṭinissaggī, yo so bhikkhū sandiṭṭhi parāmāsī hoti ādhānagāhī duppaṭinissaggī, so sattharipi agāravo viharati appatissavo, dhammepi agāravo viharati appatissavo, saŋghepi agāravo viharati appatissavo, sikkhāyapi na paripūrakāri hoti yo so bhikkhu satthari agāravo viharati appatissavo, dhamme agāravo viharati appatissavo, saŋghe agāravo viharati appatissavo, sikkhāya na paripūrakāri hoti so saŋghe vivādaɱ janeti, yo hoti vivādo bahujanaahitāya bahujanaasubāya bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaɱ evarūpaɱ ce tumhe vivādamūlaɱ ajjhattaɱ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha, tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlakassa pahānāya vāyameyyātha evarūpaɱ ce tumhe vivādamūlaɱ ajjhattaɱ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha, tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiɱ anavassavāya paṭipajjeyyātha evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa pahānaɱ hoti, evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiɱ anavassavo hoti

Punacaparaɱ bhikkhū pāpiccho hoti micchādiṭṭhi sandiṭṭhi parāmāsī hoti ādhānagāhī duppaṭinissaggī, yo so bhikkhū sandiṭṭhi parāmāsī hoti ādhānagāhī duppaṭinissaggī, so
Sattharipi agāravo viharati appatissavo, dhammepi agāravo viharati appatissavo, saŋghepi agāravo viharati appatissavo, sikkhāyapi na paripūrakāri hoti yo so bhikkhū satthari agāravo viharati appatissavo, dhamme agāravo viharati appatissavo, saŋghe agāravo viharati appatissavo, sikkhāya na paripūrakāri hoti so saŋghe vivādaɱ
[BJT Page 320] janeti, yo hoti vivādo bahujanaahitāya bahujanaasubāya bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaɱ evarūpaɱ ce tumhe vivādamūlaɱ ajjhattaɱ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha, tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlakassa pahānāya vāyameyyātha evarūpaɱ ce tumhe vivādamūlaɱ ajjhattaɱ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha, tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiɱ anavassavāya paṭipajjeyyātha evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa pahānaɱ hoti, evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiɱ anavassavo hoti

[BJT Page 322]

14. Kattha katame cha sārāṇiyā dhammā: idha bhikkhuno mettaɱ kāyakammaɱ paccupaṭṭhitaɱ hoti sabrahmacārisu āvī ceva raho ca, ayampi dhammo sārāṇiyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saŋgahāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saɱvattati.

Punacaparaɱ bhikkhuno mettaɱ vacikammaɱ paccupaṭṭhitaɱ hoti sabrahmacārīsu āvī ceva raho ca, ayampi dhammo sārāṇiyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saŋgāhāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saɱvatatti.

Punacaparaɱ bhikkhuno mettaɱ manokammaɱ paccupaṭṭhitaɱ hoti sabrahmacārīsu āvī ceva raho ca, ayampi dhammo sārāṇiyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saŋgāhāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saɱvatatti.

Punacaparaɱ bhikkhu ye te lābhā dhammikā dhammaladdhā antamaso pattapariyāpannamattampi, tathārūpehi lābhehi appaṭivibhattahogī hoti sīlavantehi sabrahmacārīhi sādhāraṇabhogī, ayampi dhammo sārāṇiyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saŋgāhāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saɱvatatti.

Punacaparaɱ bhikkhu yāni tāni sīlāni akhaṇḍāni acchiddāni asabalāni akammāsāni bhujissāni viññuppasatthāni aparāmaṭṭhāni [page 093] samādhisaɱvattanikāni, tathārūpesu sīlesu sīlasāmaññagato viharati sabrahmacārīhi āvī ceva raho ca, ayampi dhammo sārāṇiyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saŋgāhāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saɱvatatti.

Punacaparaɱ bhikkhū yāyaɱ diṭṭhi ariyā niyyānikā niyyāti takkarassa sammā dukkhakkhayāya, tathārūpāya diṭṭhiyā diṭṭhisāmaññagato viharati sabrahmacārīhi āvī ceva raho ca, ayampi dhammo sārāṇiyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saŋgāhāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saɱvatatti. Ime cha sārāṇiyā dhammā.

15. Tattha katamāni aṭṭhārasa bhedakaravatthūni: idha bhikkhu adhammaɱ dhammoti dīpeti, dhammaɱ adhammoti dīpeti, avinayaɱ vinayoti dīpeti, vinayaɱ avinayoti dīpeti, abhāsitaɱ alapitaɱ tathāgatena bhāsitaɱ lapitaɱ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, bhāsitaɱ lapitaɱ tathāgatena abhāsitaɱ alapitaɱ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, anāciṇṇaɱ tathāgatena āciṇṇaɱ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, āciṇṇaɱ tathāgatena anāciṇṇaɱ

[BJT Page 324]

Tathāgatenāti dīpeti, apaññattaɱ tathāgatena paññattaɱ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, paññattaɱ tathāgatena apaññattaɱ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, āpattiɱ anāpattīti dipeti, anāpattiɱ āpattīti dīpeti, lahukaɱ āpattiɱ garukāpattīti dipeti garukaɱ āpattiɱ lahukāpattīti dīpeti, sāvasesaɱ āpattiɱ anavasesāpattīti dīpeti, anavasseɱ āpattiɱ sāvasesāpattīti dīpeti, duṭṭhullaɱ āpattiɱ aduṭṭhullāpattīti dīpeti, aduṭaṭhullaɱ āpattiɱ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti, imāni aṭṭhārasa bhedakaravatthūni.
16. Tattha katamāni cattari adhikaraṇāni: vivādādhikaraṇaɱ, anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ, āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, kiccādhikaraṇaɱ, imāni cattāri adhikaraṇāni.

17. Tattha katame satta samathā: sammukhāvinayo, sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ, yebhuyyasikā, tassapāpiyyasikā, tiṇavatthārako ime satta samathā.
Katipucchāvāro niṭṭhito

Tassuddānaɱ:
1. Āpatti āpattikkhandhā - vinitā sattadhā puna,
Vinītāgāravā ceva - gāravā mūlameva ca.

2. Puna vinītā vipatti - samuṭṭhānā vivādanā,
Anuvādā sārānīyā - bhedādhikaraṇena ca,
Satteva samathā vuttā - padā sattarasā imeti

Cha āpattisamuṭṭhānavāro

1. Paṭhamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena pārājikaɱ āpajjeyyāti: na hīti vattabbaɱ saŋghādisesaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ thullaccayaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pācittiyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pāṭidesanīyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dukkaṭaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dubbhāsitaɱ āpajjeyyāti: na hīti vattabbaɱ.

2. Dutiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena pārājikaɱ āpajjeyyāti: na hīti vattabbaɱ saŋghādisesaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ thullaccayaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pācittiyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pāṭidesanīyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dukkaṭaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dubbhāsitaɱ āpajjeyyāti: na hīti vattabbaɱ.

[BJT Page 326]

3. Tatiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena pārājikaɱ āpajjeyyāti: na hīti vattabbaɱ saŋghādisesaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ thullaccayaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pācittiyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pāṭidesanīyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dukkaṭaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dubbhāsitaɱ āpajjeyyāti: na hīti vattabbaɱ.
[page 094]

4. Catutthena āpattisamuṭṭhānena pārājikaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ saŋghādisesaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ thullaccayaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pācittiyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pāṭidesanīyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dukkaṭaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dubbhāsitaɱ āpajjeyyāti: na hīti vattabbaɱ.

5. Pañcamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena pārājikaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ saŋghādisesaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ thullaccayaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pācittiyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pāṭidesanīyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dukkaṭaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dubbhāsitaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ.

6. Chaṭṭhena āpattisamuṭṭhānena pārājikaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ saŋghādisesaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ thullaccayaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pācittiyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ pāṭidesanīyaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dukkaṭaɱ āpajjeyyāti: siyāti vattabbaɱ dubbhāsitaɱ āpajjeyyāti: na hīti vattabbaɱ.

Cha āpattisamuṭṭhānavāro niṭṭhito paṭhamo

Katāpattivāro

1. Paṭhamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena kati āpattiyo āpajjati: paṭhamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena pañca āpattiyo āpajjati: bhikkhu kappiyasaññī saññācikāya kuṭiɱ karoti adesitavatthukaɱ pamāṇātikkantaɱ sārambhaɱ aparikkamanaɱ, payoge dukkaṭaɱ. Ekaɱ piṇḍaɱ anāgate āpatti thullaccayassa, tasmiɱ piṇḍe āgate āpatti saŋghādisesassa. Bhikkhu kappiyasaññi vikāle bhojanaɱ bhuñjati, āpatti pācittiyassa. Bhikkhu kappiyasaññī vikāle bhojanaɱ bhuñjati, āpatti pācittiyassa.Bhikkhu kappiyasaññī aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā antaragharaɱ paviṭṭhāya hatthato khādanīyaɱ vā bhojanīyaɱ vā sahatthā paṭiggahetvā bhuñjati, āpatti pāṭidesanīyassa. Paṭhamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena imā pañca āpattiyo āpajjati.

[BJT Page 328]

Tā āpatti catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ dve vipattiyo bhajanti: siyā sīlavipattiɱ siyā ācāravipattiɱ sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ pañcahi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā saŋghādisesāpattikkhandhena, siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena siyā pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandhena siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhahanti: kāyato samuṭṭhahanti, na vācato na cittato. Catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattanaɱ samathānaɱ tīhi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

2. Dutiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena kati āpattiyo āpajjati: dutiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena catasso āpattiyo āpajjati: kappiyasaññī [page 095] samādisati "kuṭiɱ me karothā"ti, tassa kuṭiɱ karonti adesitavatthukaɱ pamāṇātikkantaɱ sārambhaɱ aparikkamanaɱ, payoge dukkaṭaɱ ekaɱ piṇḍaɱ anāgate āpatti thullaccayassa. Tasmiɱ piṇḍe āgate āpatti saŋghādisesassa, bhikkhu kappiyasaññī anupasampannaɱ padasodhammaɱ vāceti, āpatti pācittiyassa dutiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena imā catasso āpattiyo āpajjati.

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpatatikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ dve vipattiyo bhajanti: siyā sīlavipattiɱ siyā ācāravipattiɱ sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ catūhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā saŋghādisesāpattikkhandhena, siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena siyā pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandhena siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhahanti: vācato samuṭṭhahanti, na kāyato na cittato. Catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattanaɱ samathānaɱ tīhi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāviyena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

3. Tatiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena kati āpattiyo āpajjati: tatiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena pañca āpattiyo āpajjati: bhikkhu kappiyasaññī saɱvidahitvā kuṭiɱ karoti, adesitavatthukaɱ pamāṇātikkantaɱ sārambhaɱ aparikkamanaɱ, payoge dukkaṭaɱ ekaɱ piṇḍaɱ anāgate āpatti thullaccayassa. Tasmiɱ piṇḍe āgate āpatti saŋghādisesassa, bhikkhu kappiyasaññī paṇītabhojanāni attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjati, āpatti pācittiyassa bhikkhu kappiyasaññī bhikkhuniyā vosāsantiyā na nivāretvā bhuñjati, āpatti pāṭidesanīyassa. Tatiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena imā pañca āpattiyo āpajjati.

[BJT Page 330]

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ dve vipattiyo bhajanti: siyā sīlavipattiɱ siyā ācāravipattiɱ sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ pañcahi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā saŋghādisesāpattikkhandhena, siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena siyā pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandhena siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhahanti: kāyato ca samuṭṭhahanti, vācato ca samuṭṭhahanti, na cittato. Catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattanaɱ samathānaɱ tīhi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

4. Catutthena āpattisamuṭṭhānena kati āpattiyo āpajjati: catutthena āpattisamuṭṭhānena cha āpattiyo āpajjati: bhikkhu methunaɱ dhammaɱ paṭisevati āpatti pārājikassa bhikkhu akappiyasaññī saññācikāya kuṭiɱ [page 096] karoti adesitavatthukaɱ pamāṇātikkantaɱ sārambhaɱ aparikkamanaɱ, payoge dukkaṭaɱ ekaɱ piṇḍaɱ anāgate āpatti thullaccayassa. Tasmiɱ piṇḍe āgate āpatti saŋghādisesassa, bhikkhu akappiyasaññī vikāle bhojanaɱ bhuñjati, āpatti pācittiyassa bhikkhū akappiyasaññī aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā antaragharaɱ paviṭṭhāya hatthato khādanīyaɱ vā bhojanīyaɱ vā sahatthā paṭiggahetvā bhuñjati, āpatti pāṭidesanīyassa. Catutthena āpattisamuṭṭhānena imā cha āpattiyo āpajjati.

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpatatikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ dve vipattiyo bhajanti: siyā sīlavipattiɱ siyā ācāravipattiɱ sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ chahi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena. Siyā siyā pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandhena siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhahanti: kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti, na vācato catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattanaɱ samathānaɱ tīhi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāviyena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

5. Pañcamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena kati āpattiyo āpajjati: pañcamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena cha āpattiyo āpajjati: bhikkhu pāpiccho icchāpakato asantaɱ abhūtaɱ uttarimanussadhammaɱ ullapati, āpatti pārājikassa bhikkhu akappiyasaññī samādiyati "kuṭiɱ me karothā"ti tassa kuṭiɱ karonti adesitavatthukaɱ pamāṇātikkantaɱ sārambhaɱ aparikkamanaɱ, payoge dukkaṭaɱ ekaɱ piṇḍaɱ anāgate āpatti thullaccayassa. Tasmiɱ piṇḍe āgate āpatti saŋghādisesassa.

[BJT Page 332]

Bhikkhu akappiyasaññī anupasampannaɱ padasodhammaɱ vāceti, āpatti pācittiyassa. Khuɱsetukāmo na vambhetukāmo na maŋkukattukāmo davakamyatyā hīnena hīnaɱ vadeti, āpatti dubbhāsitassa pañcamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena imā cha āpattiyo āpajjati.
Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ dve vipattiyo bhajanti: siyā sīlavipattiɱ siyā ācāravipattiɱ sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ chahi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena siyā saŋghādisesāpattikkhandhena, siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena. Siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena, siyā dubbhāsitāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhahanti: vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti, na kāyato catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattanaɱ samathānaɱ tihi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

6. Chaṭṭhena āpattisamuṭṭhānena kati āpattiyo āpajjati: chaṭṭhena āpattisamuṭṭhānena cha āpattiyo āpajjati: bhikkhu saɱvidahitvā bhaṇḍaɱ avaharati, āpatti [page 097] pārājikassa bhikkhu akappiyasaññī saɱvidahitvā kuṭiɱ karoti, adesitavatthukaɱ pamāṇātikkantaɱ sārambhaɱ aparikkamanaɱ, payoge dukkaṭaɱ ekaɱ piṇḍaɱ anāgate āpatti thullaccayassa. Tasmiɱ piṇḍe āgate āpatti saŋghādisesassa, bhikkhu akappiyasaññī paṇitabhojanāni attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjati, āpatti pācittiyassa bhikkhū akappiyasaññī bhikkhuniyā vosāsantiyā na nivāretvā bhuñjati, āpatti pāṭidesanīyassa chaṭṭhena āpatti samuṭṭhānena imā cha āpattiyo āpajjati.

Tā āpatti catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattinaɱ dve vipattiyo bhajanti: siyā sīlavipattiɱ siyā ācāravipattiɱ sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ chahi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena saŋghādisesāpattikkhandhena siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena siyā pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandhena siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhahanti: kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti, catunnaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattanaɱ samathānaɱ tīhi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena cāti.

Cha āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katāpattivāro niṭṭhito dutiyo

[BJT Page 334]

3. Āpattisamuṭṭhānagāthā

1. Samuṭṭhānā kāyikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena vivekadassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā kati
Pucchāmi taɱ brūhi vibhaŋgakovida.

2. Samuṭṭhānā kāyikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena vivekadassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā pañca
Etaɱ te akkhāmi vibhaŋgakovida.

3. Samuṭṭhānā vācasikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena vivekadassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā kati
Pucchāmi taɱ brūhi vibhaŋgakovida.

4. Samuṭṭhānā vācasikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena vivekadassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā catasso
Etaɱ te akkhāmi vibhaŋgakovida.

5. Samuṭṭhānā kāyikā vācasikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena vivekadassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā kati
Pucchāmi taɱ brūhi vibhaŋgakovida.

6. Samuṭṭhānā kāyikā vācasikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena viveka dassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā pañca
Etaɱ te akkhāmi vibhaŋgakovida.

7. Samuṭṭhānā kāyikā mānasikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena vivekadassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā kati
Pucchāmi taɱ brūhi vibhaŋgakovida.

8. Samuṭṭhānā kāyikā mānasikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena vivekadassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā cha
Etaɱ te akkhāmi vibhaŋgakovida.

9. Samuṭṭhānā vācasikā mānasikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena vivekadassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā kati
Pucchāmi taɱ brūhi vibhaŋgakovida.

[BJT Page 336]

10. Samuṭṭhānā vācasikā mānasikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena vivekadassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā cha
Etaɱ te akkhāmi vibhaŋgakovida.

11. Samuṭṭhānā kāyikā vācasikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena vivekadassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā kati
Pucchāmi taɱ brūhi vibhaŋgakovida.
[page 098]

12. Samuṭṭhānā kāyikā vācasikā mānasikā anantadassinā
Akkhātā lokahitena vivekadassinā,
Āpattiyo tena samuṭṭhitā cha
Etaɱ te akkhāmi vibhaŋgakovida.

Āpatti samuṭṭhānagāthā niṭṭhitā tatiyā

4. Vipatti paccayavāro

1. Sīlavipattipaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati: sīlavipattipaccayā catasso āpattiyo āpajjati: bhikkhunī jānaɱ pārājikaɱ dhammaɱ paṭicchādeti, āpatti pārājikassa vematikā paṭicchādeti, āpatti thullaccayassa bhikkhu saŋghadisesaɱ paṭicchādeti, āpatti pācittiyassa attano duṭṭhullaɱ paṭicchādeti, āpatti dukkaṭassa. Sīlavipattipaccayā imā cattasso āpattiyo āpajjati.

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ dve vipattiyo bhajanti: siyā sīlavipattiɱ siyā ācāravipattiɱ sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ catūhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhahanti: kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti, catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattanaɱ samathānaɱ tīhi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

2. Ācāravipattipaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati: ācāravipattipaccayā ekaɱ āpattiɱ āpajjati: ācāravipattiɱ paṭicchādeti, āpatti dukkaṭassa ācāravipattipaccayā imaɱ ekaɱ āpattiɱ āpajjati.

Sā āpatti catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajati: sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati:

[BJT Page 338]

Sā āpatti catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ ekaɱ vipattiɱ bhajati: ācāravipattiɱ sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ ekena āpattikkhandhena saŋgahītā: dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti: kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti. Catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattannaɱ samathānaɱ tīhi samathehi sammati: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.
3. Diṭṭhivipattipaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati: diṭṭhivipattipaccayā dve āpattiyo āpajjati: pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā yāva tatiyaɱ samanubhāsanāya nappaṭinissajjati, ñattiyā dukkaṭaɱ kamamavācāparisosāne āpatti pācittiyassa diṭṭhivipattipaccayā imā dve āpattiyo āpajjati.

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ ekaɱ vipattiɱ bhajanti: ācāravipattiɱ sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ dvīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: [page 099] siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhahanti: kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti, catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattannaɱ samathānaɱ tīhi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

4. Ājīvavipattipaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati: ājīvavipattipaccayā cha āpattiyo āpajjati: ājīvahetu ājīvakāraṇā pāpiccho icchāpakato asantaɱ abhūtaɱ uttarimanussadhammaɱ ullapati,āpatti pārājikassa. Ājīvahetu ājīvakāraṇā sañcarittaɱ samāpajjati, āpatti saŋghādisesassa ājīvahetu ājīvakāraṇā yo te vihāre vasati, so bhikkhu arahāti bhaṇati, paṭivijānantassa āpatti thullaccayassa. Ājīvahetu ājīvakāraṇā bhikkhu paṇitabhojanāni attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjati, āpatti pācittiyassa. Ājīvahetu ājīvakāraṇā bhikkhunī paṇītabhojanāni attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjati, āpatti pāṭidesanīyassa. Ājīvahetu ājivakāraṇā sūpaɱ vā odanaɱ vā agilāno attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjati āpatti dukkaṭassa ājīvavipattipaccayā imā cha āpattiyo āpajjati.

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ dve vipattiyo bhajanti: siyā sīlavipatti, siyā ācāravipattiɱ sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ chahi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena siyā saŋghādisesāpattikkhandhena siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena.
[BJT Page 340]

Siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena siyā pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandhena siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: siyā kāyato samuṭṭhahanti na vācato na cittato siyā vācato samuṭṭhahanti, na kāyato na cittato siyā kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhahanti, na cittato. Siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti na vācato, siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti, na kāyato, siyā kāyato ca vācato ca citatto ca samuṭṭhahanti catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattanaɱ samathānaɱ tīhi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

Vipattipaccayavāro niṭṭhito catuttho

5. Adhikaraṇa paccayavāro

1. Vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati: vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā dve āpattiyo āpajjati: upasampannaɱ omasati, āpatti pācittiyassa. Anupasampannaɱ omasati, āpatti dukkaṭassa. Vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā imā dve āpattiyo āpajjati.
Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ ekaɱ vipattiɱ bhajanti: ācāra vipattiɱ, sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ dvīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena. Siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhanti: siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti na vācato. Siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti, na [page 100] kāyato. Siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti. Catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattannaɱ samathānaɱ tīhi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

2. Anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati: anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā tisso āpattiyo āpajjati: bhikkhuɱ amūlakena pārājikena dhammena anuddhaɱseti āpatti saŋghādisesassa amūlakena saŋghādisesena anuddhaɱseti āpatti pācittiyassa. Amūlakāya ācāravipattiyā anuddhaɱseti āpatti dukkaṭassa. Anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā imā tisso āpattiyo āpajjati.

[BJT Page 342]

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ dve vipattiyo bhajanti: siyā sīlavipattiɱ siyā ācāravipattiɱ, sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ tīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā saŋghādisesāpattikkhandhena siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena. Siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti na vācato. Siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti, na kāyato. Siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti. Catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattannaɱ samathānaɱ tīhi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

3. Āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati: āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā catasso āpattiyo āpajjati: bhikkhunī jānaɱ pārājikaɱ dhammaɱ paṭicchādeti, āpatti pārājikassa. Vematikā paṭicchādeti. Āpatti thullaccayassa. Bhikkhu saŋghādisesaɱ paṭicchādeti āpattipācittiyassa ācāravipattiɱ paṭicchādeti āpatti dukkaṭassa āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā imā catasso āpattiyo āpajjati.

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ dve vipattiyo bhajanti: siyā sīlavipattiɱ siyā ācāravipattiɱ, sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ catūhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena. Siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena. Siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. Channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhahanti: kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti. Catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattannaɱ samathānaɱ tihi samathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

4. Kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati: kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā pañca āpattiyo āpajjati: ukkhittānuvattikā bhikkhunī yāvatatiyaɱ samanubhāsanāya nappaṭinissajjati, ñattiyā dukkaṭaɱ. Dvīhi kammavācāhi thullaccayā, kammavācāpariyosāne āpatti pārājikassa. Bhedakānuvattakā bhikkhū yāvatatiyaɱ samanubhāsanāya nappaṭinissajjanti. Āpatti saŋghādisesassa. Pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā yāvatatiyaɱ samanubhāsanāya nappaṭinissajati, āpatti pācittiyassa. Kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā imā pañca āpattiyo āpajjati.

[BJT Page 344]
[page 101]

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti: sattannaɱ āpatatikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti: catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ: sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti:

Tā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ dve vipattiyo bhajanti: siyā sīlavipattiɱ siyā ācāravipattiɱ, sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ pañcahi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena. Siyā saŋghādisesāpattikkhandhena. Siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena. Siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. Channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhahanti: kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhahanti. Catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ āpattādhikaraṇaɱ, sattannaɱ samathānaɱ tīhisamathehi sammanti: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

Ṭhapetvā satta āpattiyo sattāpattikkhandhe avasesā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ kati vipattiyo bhajanti, sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ katīhi āpattikkhandhehi saŋgahītā, channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ katīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhahanti, catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ, sattannaɱ samathānaɱ katīhi samathehi sammanti.

Ṭhapetvā satta āpattiyo sattāpattikkhandhe avasesā āpattiyo catunnaɱ vipattīnaɱ na katamaɱ vipattiɱ bhajanti, sattannaɱ āpattikkhandhānaɱ na katamena āpattikkhandhena saŋgahītā, channaɱ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaɱ na katamena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhahanti, catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ na katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ, sattannaɱ samathānaɱ na katamena samathena sammanti. Taɱ tissa hetu: ṭhapetvā sattāpattikkhandhe natthaññāpattiyoti.

Adhikaraṇapaccayavāro niṭṭhito pañcamo.

Antarapeyyālo 1- niṭṭhito

Tassuddānaɱ:
Kati pucchā samuṭṭhānā - katāpatti tatheva ca,
Samuṭṭhānā vipattī ca - tathādhikaraṇena cāti.

1. Antarapeyyālaɱ - sīmu.

[BJT Page 346]

Samathabhedo
6. Pariyāyavāro

1. Vivādādhikaraṇassa kiɱ pubbaŋgamaɱ, kati ṭhānāni, kati vatthūni, kati bhumiyo, kati hetu, kati mūlāni, katīhākārehi vivadati, vivādādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati.

2. Anuvādādhikaraṇassa kiɱ pubbaŋgamaɱ, kati ṭhānāni, kati vatthūni, kati bhumiyo, kati hetu, kati mūlāni, katīhākārehi anuvadati, anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati.
3. Āpattādhikaraṇassa kiɱ pubbaŋgamaɱ, kati ṭhānāni, kati vatthūni, kati bhumiyo, kati hetu, kati mūlāni, katīhākārehi āpattiɱ āpajjati, āpattādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati.

4. Kiccādhikaraṇassa kiɱ pubbaŋgamaɱ, kati ṭhānāni, kati vatthūni, kati bhumiyo, kati hetu, kati mūlāni, katīhākārehi kiccaɱ jāniyā, kiccādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati.
[page 102]
1. Vivādādhikaraṇassa kiɱ pubbaŋgamanti: lobho pubbaŋgamo, doso pubbaŋgamo, moho pubbaŋgamo alobho pubbaŋgamo, adoso pubbaŋgamo. Amoho pubbaŋgamo. Kati ṭhānānīti: aṭṭhārasa bhedakaravatthūni ṭhānāni. Kati vatthūnīti: aṭṭhārasa bhedakara vatthūni vatthūni. Kati bhumiyoti: aṭṭhārasa bhedakaravatthūni bhumiyo. Kati hetūti: nava hetu: tayo kusalahetu, tayo akusalahetu, tayo abyākatahetu. Kati mulānīti: dvādasa mūlānī. Katihākārehi vivadatīti: dvihākārehi vivadati: dhammadiṭṭhi vā, adhammadiṭṭhi vā. Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammatīti; vivādādhikaraṇaɱ dvīhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca

2. Anuvādādhikaraṇassa kiɱ pubbaŋgamanti: lobho pubbaŋgamo, doso pubbaŋgamo, moho pubbaŋgamo alobho pubbaŋgamo, adoso pubbaŋgamo. Amoho pubbaŋgamo. Kati ṭhānānīti: catasso vipattiyo ṭhānāni, kati vatthunīti: catasso vipattiya vatthūni. Kati bhumiyoti: catasso vipattiyo bhumiyo, kati hetūti: nava hetu: tayo kusalahetu, tayo akusalahetu, tayo abyākatahetu. Kati mulānīti: cuddasa mūlāni. Katīhākārehi anuvadatīti: dvihākārehi anuvadati: vatthuto vā āpattito vā anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammatīti; anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ catūhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca

Piṭavu 348

3. Āpattādhikaraṇassa kiɱ pubbaŋgamanti: lobho pubbaŋgamo, doso pubbeŋgamo, moho pubbaŋgamo alobho pubbaŋgamo, adoso pubbaŋgamo. Amoho pubbaŋgamo. Kati ṭhānānīti: sattapāttikkhandhā ṭhānāni. Kati vatthūnīti: sattāpattikkhandhā vatthūni: kati bhumiyoti: sattāpattikkhandhā bhumiyo, kati hetuti: nava hetu: 1- tayo kusalahetu, tayo akusalahetu, tayo abyākatahetu. Kati mulānīti: cha āpattisamuṭṭhānāni mūlāni. Katīhākārehi āpattiɱ āpajjati: chahākārehi āpattiɱ āpajajati: alajjitā, aññāṇatā, kukkuccāpakatatā, akappiye kappiyasaññitā, kappiye akappiyasaññitā, sati sammosā āpattādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammatīti: āpattidhiraṇaɱ tīhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

4. Kiccādhikaraṇassa kiɱ pubbaŋgamanti: lobho pubbaŋgamo, doso pubbeŋgamo, moho pubbaŋgamo alobho pubbaŋgamo, adoso pubbaŋgamo. Amoho pubbaŋgamo. Kati ṭhānānīti: cattāri kammāni ṭhānāni. Kati vatthūnīti: cattāri kammāni vatthūni. Kati bhumiyoti: cattāri kammāni bhumiyo, kati hetūti: nava hetu: tayo kusalahetu, tayo akusalahetu, tayo abyākatahetu. Kati mulānīti: ekaɱ mūlaɱ saŋgho. Katīhākārehi kiccaɱ jāyatīti: dvihākārehi kiccaɱ jāyati: ñattito vā, apalokanato vā kiccādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammatīti: kiccādhikaraṇaɱ ekena samathena sammati: sammukhāvinayena.
[page 103]

Kati samathā: satta samathā: sammukhāvinayo, sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ, yebhuyyasikā, tassapāpiyyasikā, tiṇavatthārako.

Ime satta samathā. Siyā ime satta samathā dasa samathā honti. Dasa samathā satta samathā honti. Vatthuvasena pariyāyena siyāti.

Kathañca siyā: vivādādhikaraṇassa dve samathā. Anuvādādhikaraṇassa cattāro samathā, āpattādhikaraṇassa tayo samathā, kiccādhikaraṇassa eko samatho. Evaɱ ime satta samathā dasasamathā honti. Dasa samathā satta samathā honti vatthuvasena pariyāyena.

Pariyāyavāro niṭṭhito chaṭṭho

1. Tatihetuti chahetu - machasaɱ

[BJT Page 350] [\x 35/]

7. Sādhāraṇavāro

Kati samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā, kati samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā kati samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā, kati samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā. Kati samathā apatattādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā, kati samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā. Kati samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā, kati samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā.

1. Dve samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā: sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā. Pañca samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā: sativinayo amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ, tassapāpiyyasikā, tiṇavatthārako

2. Cattāro samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā: sammukhāvinayo sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, tassapāpiyyasikā tayo samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā: yebhuyyasikā paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ, tiṇavatthārako

3. Tayo samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā: sammukhāvinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ tiṇavatthārako cattāro samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā, yebhuyyasikā sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, tassa pāpiyyasikā

4. Eko samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā: sammukhāvinayo cha samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā, yebhuyyasikā sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ, tassapāpiyyasikā, tiṇavatthārako.
Sādhāraṇavāro niṭṭhito sattamo

8. Tabbhāgiyavāro

Kati samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā, kati samathā vivādādhīkaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā. Kati samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā, kati samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā. Kati samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā, kati samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā. Kati samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā, kati samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā.
[page 104]

1. Dve samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā: sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā. Pañca samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā: sativinayo amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ, tassapāpiyyasikā, tiṇavatthārako

2. Cattāro samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā: sammukhāvinayo sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, tassapāpiyyasikā tayo samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā: yebhuyyasikā paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ, tiṇavatthārako

[BJT Page 352]

3. Tayo samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā: sammukhāvinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ tiṇavatthārako cattāro samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā: yebhuyyasikā sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, tassa pāpiyyasikā

4. Eko samatho kiccādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā: sammukhāvinayo cha samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā: yebhuyyasikā sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ, tassapāpiyyasikā, tiṇavatthārako

Tabbhāgiyavāro niṭṭhito aṭṭhamo

9. Samathā samathassa sādhāraṇavāro

Samathā samathassa sādhāraṇā, samathā samathassa asādhāraṇa, siyā samathā samathassa sādhāraṇā, siyā samathā samathassa asādhāraṇā.

Kathaɱ siyā samathā samathassa sādhāraṇā, kathaɱ siyā samathā samathassa āsādhāraṇā:

1. Yebhuyyasikā sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇā, sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa asādhāraṇā.

2. Sativinayo sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇo, amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya asādhāraṇo.

3. Amūḷhavinayo sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇo, paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa asādhāraṇo.

4. Paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇaɱ tassapāpiyyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa asādhāraṇaɱ.

5. Tassapāpiyyasikāya sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇā, tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa asādhāraṇā.

6. Tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇo, yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyyasikāya asādhāraṇo; evaɱ siyā samathā samathassa sādhāraṇā evaɱ siyā samathā samathassa asādhāraṇā.

Samathā samathassa sādhāraṇavāro niṭṭhito navamo.

[BJT Page 354]

10. Samathā samathassa tabbhāgiyavāro

Samathā samathassa tabbhāgiyā, samathā samathassa aññabhāgiyā siyā samathā samathassa tabbhāgiyā, siyā samathā samathassa aññabhāgiyā.

Kathaɱ siyā samathā samathassa tabbhāgiyā, kathaɱ siyā samathā samathassa aññabhāgiyā:

1. Yebhuyyasikā sammukhāvinayassa tabbhāgiyā, sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa aññabhāgiyā.

2. Sativinayo sammukhāvinayassa tabbhāgiyo, amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya aññabhāgiyo.

3. Amūḷhavinayo sammukhāvinayassa tabbāgiyo, paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa aññabhāgiyo.

4. Paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ sammukhāvinayassa tabbāgiyaɱ tassapāpiyyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa aññabhāgiyaɱ.

5. Tassapāpiyyasikāya sammukhāvinayassa tabbābhāgiyā, tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyyasikāya aññabhāgiyā.

6. Tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayassa tabbhāgiyo, yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyyasikāya aññabhāgiyo; evaɱ siyā samathā samathassa tabbhāgiyā. Evaɱ siyā samathā samathassa aññabhāgiyā.

Samathā samathassa tabbhāgiyavāro niṭṭhito dasamo.

11. Samathāsammukhāvinayavāro

Samathā sammukhāvinayo. Sammukhāvinayo samatho. Samatho yebhuyyasikā, yebhuyyasikā samatho. Samatho [page 105] sativinayo. Sativinayo samatho. Samatho amūḷhavinayo. Amūḷhavinayo samatho. Samatho paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ. Paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ samatho. Samatho tassapāpiyyasikā, tassapāpiyyasikā samatho. Samatho tiṇavatthārako, tiṇavatthārako samatho.
1. Yebhuyyasikā sativinayo amūḷhavinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ tassapāpiyyasikā tiṇavatthārako ime samathā samathā. No sammukhā vinayo. Sammukhāvinayo samatho ceva sammukhāvinayo ca.

2. Sativinayo amūḷhavinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ tassapāpiyyasikā tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayo ime samathā samathā, no yebhuyyasikā. Yebhuyyasikā samatho ceva yebhuyyasikā ca.

[BJT Page 356]

3. Amūḷhavinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ tassapāpiyyasikā tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā ime samathā samathā, no sativinayo. Sativinayo samatho ceva sativinayo ca.
4. Paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ tassapāpiyyasikā tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā sativinayo ime samathā samathā. No amūḷhavinayo. Amūḷhavinayo samatho ceva amūḷha vinayo ca.
.
5. Tassapāpiyyasikā tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā sativinayo amūḷhavinayo ime samathā samathā, no paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ. Paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ samatho ceva paṭiññātakaraṇañca.
.
6. Tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā sativinayo amūḷhavinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ ime samathā samathā, no tassāpiyyasikā. Tassapāpiyyasikā samatho ceva tassapāpiyyasikā ca.

7. Sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā sativinayo amūḷhavinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ tassapāpiyyasikā ime samathā samathā, no tiṇavatthārako. Tiṇavatthārako samatho ceva tiṇavatthārako ca.
.
Samathasammukhāvinayavāro niṭṭhito ekādasamo

12. Vinayavāro

Vinayo sammukhāvinayo. Sammukhāvinayo vinayo. Vinayo yebhuyyasikā. Yebhuyyasikā vinayo. Vinayo sativinayo, sativinayo vinayo. Vinayo amūḷhavinayo, amūḷhavinayo vinayo. Vinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ. Paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ vinayo. Vinayo tassapāpiyyasikā. Tassapāpiyyasikā vinayo. Vinayo tiṇavatthārako. Tiṇavatthārako vinayo.

1. Vinayo siyā sammukhāvinayo. Siyā na sammukhāvinayo. Sammukhāvinayo vinayo ceva sammukhāvinayo ca.

2. Vinayo siyā yebhuyyasikā. Siyā na yebhuyyasikā. Yebhuyyasikā vinayo ceva yebhuyyasikā ca.

3. Vinayo siyā sativinayo. Siyā na sativinayo sativinayo vinayo ceva sativinayo ca.
4. Vinayo siyā amūḷhavinayo. Siyā na amūḷhavinayo. Amūḷhavinayo vinayo ceva amūḷhavinayo ca.

5. Vinayo siyā paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ siyā na paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ vinayo ceva paṭiññātakaraṇañca.

[BJT Page 358]

6. Vinayo siyā tassapāpiyyasikā siyā na tassapāpiyyasikā. Tassapāpiyyasikā vinayo ceva tassapāpiyyasikā ca.

7. Vinayo siyā tiṇavatthārako. Siyā na tiṇavatthārako. Tiṇavatthārako vinayo ceva tiṇavatthārako ca.

Vinayavāro niṭṭhito dvāsadamo

13. Kusalavāro

Sammukhāvinayo kusalo akusalo abyākato. Yebhuyyasikā kusalā akusalā abyākatā. Sativinayo kusalo akusalo abyākato. Amūḷhavinayo kusalo akusalo abyākato, paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ kusalaɱ akusalaɱ abyākataɱ, tassapāpiyyāsikā kusalā akusalā abyākatā. Tiṇavatthārako kusalo akusalo abyākato.

1. Sammukhāvinayo siyā kusalo siyā abyākato. Natthi sammukhā vinayo akusalo.
2. Yebhuyyasikā siyā kusalā. Siyā akusalā. Siyā abyākatā.
.
3. Sativinayo siyā kusalo. Siyā akusalo. Siyā abyākato.

4. Amūḷhavinayo siyā kusalo. Siyā akusalo. Siyā abyākato.

5. Paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ siyā kusalaɱ. Siyā akusalaɱ. Siyā abyākataɱ.

6. Tassapāpiyyasikā siyā kusalā. Siyā akusalā. Siyā abyākatā.

7. Tiṇavatthārako siyā kusalo. Siyā akusalo. Siyā abyākato.
[page 106]

Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ kusalaɱ akusalaɱ abyākataɱ. Anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ kusalaɱ akusalaɱ abyākataɱ. Āpattādhikaraṇaɱ kusalaɱ akusalaɱ abyākataɱ. Kiccādhikaraṇaɱ kusalaɱ akusalaɱ abyākataɱ:
1. Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ siyā kusalaɱ. Siyā akusalaɱ. Siyā abyākataɱ.

2. Anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ siyā kusalaɱ. Siyā akusalaɱ. Siyā abyākataɱ.

3. Āpattādhikaraṇaɱ siyā akusalaɱ. Siyā siyā abyākataɱ. Natthi āpattādhikaraṇaɱ kusalaɱ.
4. Kiccādhikaraṇaɱ siyā kusalaɱ. Siyā akusalaɱ. Siyā abyākataɱ.

Kusalavāro niṭṭhito terasamo.

[BJT Page 360]

14. Yatthavāro

1. Yattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati, tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati. Yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha yebhuyyasiyā labbhati. Na tattha sativinayo labbhati. Na tattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati. Na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati. Na ttatha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati.

2. Yattha sativinayo labbhati, tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati. Yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha yebhuyyasiyā labbhati. Na tattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati. Na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati. Na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati. Na tattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati.

3. Yattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati, tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati. Yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati. Na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati. Na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati. Na tattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha sativinayo labbhati.

4. Yattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati, tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati. Yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati. Na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati. Na tattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha sativinayo labbhati. Na tattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati.

5. Yattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati, tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati. Yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati. Na tattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha sativinayo labbhati. Na ttatha amūḷhavinayo labbhati. Na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati.

6. Yattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati, tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati. Yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati. Na tattha yebhuyasikā labbhati. Na tattha
Sativinayo labbhati. Na tattha amulhavinayo labbhati. Na ttatha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati. Na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati.

7. Yattha yebhuyyasikā tattha sammukhāvinayo. Yattha sammukhāvinayo tattha yebhuyyasikā. Na tattha sativinayo. Na tattha amūḷhavinayo. Na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ. Na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako.

8. Yattha sativinayo, tattha sammukhāvinayo yattha sammukhāvinayo tattha sativinayo na ttatha amūḷhavinayo na ttatha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ. Na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako. Na tattha yebhuyyasikā ( sammukhāvinayaɱ kātunamūlaɱ - pe - )

[BJT Page 362]

9. Yattha tiṇavatthārako, tattha sammukhāvinayo yattha sammukhāvinayo tattha tiṇavatthārako na ttatha yebhuyyasikā na tattha sativinayo na tattha amūḷhavinayo na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā

Cakkapeyyālaɱ
Yatthavāro niṭṭhito cuddasamo.

15. Samathavāro

1. Yasmiɱ samaye sammukhā vinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca adhikaraṇaɱ vūpasammati, yattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati. Tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha sativinayo labbhati. Na tattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati. Na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati. Na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati.
[page 107]

2. Yasmiɱ samaye sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca adhikaraṇaɱ vūpasammati, yattha sativinayo labbhati. Tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha sativinayo labbhati. Na tattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati. Na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati. Na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati. Na tattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati.

3. Yasmiɱ samaye sammukhāvinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca adhikaraṇaɱ vūpasammati, yattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati. Tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati. Na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati, na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati. Na tattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha sativinayo labbhati.

4. Yasmiɱ samaye sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca adhikaraṇaɱ vūpasammati, yattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati. Tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati. Na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati. Na tattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha sativinayo labbhati. Na tattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati.
5. Yasmiɱ samaye sammukhāvinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca adhikaraṇaɱ vupasammati, yattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati. Tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati. Na tattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha sativinayo labbhati. Na tattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati. Na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati.

[BJT Page 364]

6. Yasmiɱ samaye sammukhāvinayona ca tiṇavatthārakena ca adhikaraṇaɱ vupasammati, yattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati. Tattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, yattha sammukhāvinayo labbhati, tattha tiṇavatthārako labbhati. Na tattha yebhuyyasikā labbhati. Na tattha sativinayo labbhati. Na tattha amūḷhavinayo labbhati. Na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ labbhati. Na tattha tassapāpiyyasikā labbhati.

Samathavāro niṭṭhito paṇṇarasamo.

16. Saɱsaṭṭhavāro

Adhikaraṇanti vā samathāti vā ime dhammā saɱsaṭṭhā udāhu visaɱsaṭṭhā, labbhā ca panimesaɱ dhammānaɱ vinibbhujitvā vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaɱ paññāpetunti:

Adhikaraṇanti vā samathāti vā ime dhammā visaɱsaṭṭhā, no saɱsaṭṭhā. Labbhā ca panimesaɱ dhammānaɱ vinibbhujitvā vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaɱ. Paññāpetunti, so mā hevantissa vacanīyo. Adhikaraṇanti vā samathāti vā ime dhammā saɱsaṭṭhā no visaɱsaṭṭhā na ca labbhā 1imesaɱ dhammānaɱ vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaɱ paññāpetuɱ. Taɱ kissa hetu: nanu vuttaɱ bhagavatā "cattārimāni bhikkhave adhikaraṇāni, satta samathā. Adhikaraṇā samathehi sammanti. Samathā adhikaraṇehi sammantī"ti. Evaɱ ime dhammā saɱsaṭṭhā no visaɱsaṭṭhā no ca labbhā imesaɱ dhammānaɱ vinibbhujitvā vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaɱ paññāpetunti.

Saɱsaṭṭhavāro niṭṭhito soḷasamo.

17. Sammativāro

Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati, āpattādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati, kiccādhīkaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati:

1. Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ dvīhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca.

2. Anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ catūhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca.

3. Āpattādhikaraṇaɱ tīhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

4. Kiccādhikaraṇaɱ ekena samathena sammati: sammukhāvinayena.

1. No ca labbhā - machasaɱ

[BJT Page 366]

1. Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca pañcahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca.
[page 108]

2. Vivādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: vivādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca catūhi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

3. Vivādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: vivādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca dvīhi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca
4. Anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca chahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca

5. Anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca catūhi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca.

6. Āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca tīhi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

7. Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca sattahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

8. Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca pañcahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca.

9. Anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca chahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

[BJT Page 368]

10. Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattadhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca sattahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikhāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

Sammativāro 1- niṭṭhito sattarasamo.

18. Sammati na sammativāro

Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati, katīhi samathehi na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati, katīhi samathehi na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati, katīhi samathehi na sammati, kiccādhikaraṇaɱ katīhi samathehi sammati, katīhi samathehi na sammati,
1. Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ dvīhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikhāya ca. Pañcahi samathehi na sammati: sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

2. Anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ catūhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca. Amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca. Tīhi samathehi na sammati: yebhuyyasikāya ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

3. Āpattādhikaraṇaɱ tīhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca, catūhi samathehi na sammati: yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca.
[page 109]

4. Kiccādhikaraṇaɱ ekena samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena chahi samathehi na sammati: yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

5. Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikarañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: katīhi samathehi na sammanti: vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca pañcahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca dvīhi samathehi na sammanti: paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

1. Samantivāro - machasaɱ

[BJT Page 370]

6. Vivādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: katīhi samathehi na sammanti: vivādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca catūhi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca tīhi samathehi na sammanti: sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca.

7. Vivādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: katīhi samathehi na sammanti: vivādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca dvīhi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca pañcahi samathehi na sammanti: sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

8. Anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: katīhi samathehi na sammanti: anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca chahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. Ekena samathena na sammanti yebhuyyasikāya.

9. Anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikarañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: katīhi samathehi na sammanti: anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca catūhi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tīhi samathehi na sammanti: yebhuyyasikāya ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

10 Āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: katīhi samathehi na sammanti: āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca tīhi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. Catūhi samathehi na sammanti: yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca

11. Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: katīhi samathehi na sammanti: vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca sattahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.
12. Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: katīhi samathehi na sammanti: vivādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca pañcahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca. Dvīhi samathehi na sammanti: paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.
[BJT Page 372]

13. Anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: katīhi samathehi na sammanti: anuvādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca chahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca ekena samathena na sammanti: yebhuyyasikāya.
14. Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katīhi samathehi sammanti: katīhi samathehi na sammanti: vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca sattahi samathehi sammanti: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

Sammati na sammati vāro niṭṭhito aṭṭhārasamo.

19. Samathādhikaraṇavāro

Samathā samathehi sammanti, samathā adhikaraṇehi sammanti. Adhikaraṇā samathehi sammanti adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi sammanti:
[page 110]

Siyā samathā samathehi sammanti. Siyā samathā samathehi na sammanti. Siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi sammanti. Siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti. Siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi sammanti. Siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi na sammanti. Siyā adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi sammanti. Siyā adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti.

(1)
Kathaɱ siyā samathā samathehi sammanti, kathaɱ siyā samathā samathehi na sammanti:

Yebhuyyasikā sammukhāvinayena sammati. Sativinayena na sammati. Amūḷhavinayena na sammati. Paṭiññātakaraṇena na sammati. Tassapāpiyyasikāya na sammati.

Sativinayo sammukhāvinayena sammati. Amūḷhavinayena na sammati. Paṭiññātakaraṇena na sammati. Tassapāpiyyasikāya na sammati. Tiṇavatthārakena na sammati. Yebhuyyasikāya na sammati.
Amūḷhavinayo sammukhāvinayena sammati. Paṭiññātakaraṇena na sammati. Tassapāpiyyasikāya na sammati. Tiṇavatthārakena na sammati. Yebhuyyasikāya na sammati. Sativinayena na sammati.

Paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ sammukhāvinayena sammati. Tassapāpiyyasikāya na sammati. Tiṇavatthārakena na sammati. Yebhuyyasikāya na sammati. Sativinayena na sammati. Amūḷhavinayena na sammati.
[BJT Page 374]

Tassapāpiyyasikā sammukhāvinayena sammati. Tiṇavatthārakena na sammati. Yebhuyyasikāya na sammati. Sativinayena na sammati. Amūḷhavinayena na sammati. Paṭiññātakaraṇena na sammati.

Tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayena sammati. Yebhuyyasikāya na sammati. Sativinayena na sammati. Amūḷhavinayena na sammati. Paṭiññātakaraṇena na sammati. Tassapāpiyyasikāya na sammati.

Evaɱ siyā samathā samathehi sammanti. Evaɱ siyā samathā samathehi na sammanti.

(2)
Kathaɱ siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi sammanti, kathaɱ siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti:

Sammukhāvinayo vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati. Kiccādhikaraṇena sammati.

Yebhuyyasikā vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati. Kiccādhikaraṇena sammati.

Sativinayo vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati. Kiccādhikaraṇena sammati.

Amūḷhavinayo vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati. Kiccādhikaraṇena sammati.

Paṭiññātakaraṇaɱ vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati. Kiccādhikaraṇena sammati.

Tassapāpiyyasikā vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati. Kiccādhikaraṇena sammati.

Tiṇavatthārako vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati. Kiccādhikaraṇena sammati.

Evaɱ siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi sammanti. Evaɱ siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti.

(3)
Kathaɱ siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi sammanti, kathaɱ siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi na sammanti.

Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca sammati. Sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca na sammati.

[BJT Page 376]

Anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ sammukhāviyena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca sammati. Yebhuyyasikāya ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca na sammati.

Āpattādhikaraṇaɱ sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca sammati. Yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca na sammati.

Kiccādhikaraṇaɱ sammukhāvinayena sammati. Yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca [page 111] tassapāpiyyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca na sammati.

Evaɱ siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi sammanti. Evaɱ siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi na sammanti.

(4)
Kathaɱ adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi sammanti, kathaɱ siyā adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti.

Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati. Kiccādhikaraṇena sammati.

Anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati. Kiccādhikaraṇena sammati.

Āpattādhikaraṇaɱ vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati. Kiccādhikaraṇena sammati.

Kiccādhikaraṇaɱ vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati. Anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati. Kiccādhikaraṇena sammati.

Evaɱ siyā adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi sammanti. Evaɱ siyā adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti
Chapi samathā cattāropi adhikaraṇā sammukhāvinayena sammanti. Sammukhāvinayo na kenaci sammati

Samathādhikaraṇavāro niṭṭhito ekunavīsatimo

20. Samuṭṭhāpanavāro

1. Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ samuṭṭhāpeti: vivādādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ na katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ samuṭṭhāpeti. Api ca vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. Yathākathaɱ viya: idha bhikkhū vivadanti dhammoti vā adhammoti vā vinayoti vā avinayoti vā bhāsitaɱ lapitaɱ tathāgatenāti vā abhāsitaɱ alapitaɱ tathāgatenāti vā, āciṇṇaɱ

[BJT Page 378]

Tathāgatenāti vā anāciṇṇaɱ tathāgatenāti vā, paññattaɱ tathāgatenāti vā apaññattaɱ tathāgatenāti vā, āpattīti vā anāpattīti vā, lahukāpattīti vā, garukāpattīti vā, sāvasesāpattīti vā anavasesāpattīti vā, duṭṭhullāpattīti vā aduṭṭhullāpattīti vā. Yaɱ tattha bhaṇḍanaɱ kalaho viggaho vivādo nānāvādo aññathāvādo vipaccayatāya vohāro medhagaɱ idaɱ vuccati vivādādhikaraṇaɱ. Vivādādhikaraṇe saŋgho vivadati, vivādādhikaraṇaɱ. Vivadamāno anuvadati, anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ, anuvadamāno āpattiɱ āpajjati, āpattādhikaraṇaɱ tāya āpattiyā saŋgho kammaɱ karoti, kiccādhikaraṇaɱ. Evaɱ vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti.

2. Anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ samuṭṭhāpeti: anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ na katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ samuṭṭhāpeti. Api ca anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. Yathākathaɱ viya: idha bhikkhū bhikkhuɱ anuvadanti sīlavipattiyā vā, ācāravipattiyā vā diṭṭhivipattiyā vā ājīvavipattiyā vā yo tattha anuvādo anuvadanā anullapanā anubhaṇanā anusampavaŋkatā abbhussahanatā anubalappadānaɱ, idaɱ vuccati anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ anuvādādhikaraṇe saŋgho vivadati, vivādādhikaraṇaɱ vivādamāno anuvadati anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ. Anuvadamāno āpattiɱ apajjati, āpattādhikaraṇaɱ. Tāya āpattiyā saŋgho kammaɱ karoti, kiccādhikaraṇaɱ. Evaɱ anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti.

3. Āpattādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ samuṭṭhāpeti: āpattādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ na katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ samuṭṭhāpeti. Api ca āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. Yathākathaɱ viya: pañcapi āpattikkhandhā sattapi āpattikkhandhā āpattādhikaraṇaɱ. Idaɱ vuccati āpattādhikaraṇaɱ āpattādhikaraṇe saŋgho vivadati, vivādādhikaraṇaɱ. Vivadamāno [page 112] anuvadati, anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ. Anuvadamāno āpattiɱ āpajjati, āpattādhikaraṇaɱ. Tāya āpattiyā saŋgho kammaɱ karoti kiccādhikaraṇaɱ evaɱ āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti.

4. Kiccādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ samuṭṭhāpeti: kiccādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ na katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ samuṭṭhāpeti. Api ca kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. Yathākathaɱ viya: yā saŋghassa kiccayatā karaṇīyatā apalokanakammaɱ ñattikammaɱ ñattidutiyakammaɱ ñatatticatutthakammaɱ, idaɱ vuccati kiccādhikaraṇaɱ kiccādhikaraṇe saŋgho vivadati, vivādādhikaraṇaɱ vivadamāno anuvadati, anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ. Anuvadamāno āpattiɱ āpajjati, āpattādhikaraṇaɱ. Tāya āpattiyā saŋgho kammaɱ karoti kiccādhikaraṇaɱ. Evaɱ kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti.

Samuṭṭhāpanavāro niṭṭhito visatimo

[BJT Page 380]

21. Bhajativāro

1. Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ bhajati, katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ upanissitaɱ, katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ pariyāpannaɱ, katamena adhikaraṇena saŋgahītaɱ.

2. Anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ bhajati, katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ upanissitaɱ, katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ pariyāpannaɱ, katamena adhikaraṇena saŋgahītaɱ.

3. Āpattādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ bhajati, katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ upanissitaɱ, katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ pariyāpannaɱ, katamena adhikaraṇena saŋgahītaɱ.

4. Kiccādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ bhajati, katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ upanissitaɱ, katamaɱ adhikaraṇaɱ pariyāpannaɱ, katamena adhikaraṇena saŋgahītaɱ.

1. Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ vivādādhikaraṇaɱ bhajati, vivādādhikaraṇaɱ upanissitaɱ, vivādādhikaraṇaɱ pariyāpannaɱ, vivādādhikaraṇena saŋgahītaɱ.

2. Anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ bhajati, anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ upanissitaɱ, anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ pariyāpannaɱ, anuvādādhikaraṇena saŋgahītaɱ.

3. Āpattādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ apattādhikaraṇaɱ bhajati, āpattādhikaraṇaɱ upanissitaɱ, āpattādhikaraṇaɱ pariyāpannaɱ, āpattādhikaraṇena saŋgahītaɱ.

4. Kiccādhikaraṇaɱ catunnaɱ adhikaraṇānaɱ kiccādhikaraṇaɱ bhajati, kiccādhikaraṇaɱ
Upanissitaɱ, kiccādhikaraṇaɱ pariyāpannaɱ, kiccādhikaraṇena saŋgahītaɱ.

1. Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ sattannaɱ samathānaɱ kati samathe bhajati, kati samathe upanissitaɱ, kati samathe pariyāpannaɱ, katīhi samathehi saŋgahītaɱ, katīhi samathehi sammati.

2. Anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ sattannaɱ samathānaɱ kati samathe bhajati, kati samathe upanissitaɱ, kati samathe pariyāpannaɱ, katīhi samathehi saŋgahītaɱ, katīhi samathehi sammati.

3. Āpattādhikaraṇaɱ sattannaɱ samathānaɱ kati samathe bhajati, kati samathe upanissitaɱ, kati samathe pariyāpannaɱ, katīhi samathehi saŋgahītaɱ, katīhi samathehi sammati.

4. Kiccādādhikaraṇaɱ sattannaɱ samathānaɱ kati samathe bhajati, kati samathe upanissitaɱ, kati samathe pariyāpannaɱ, katīhi samathehi saŋgahītaɱ, katīhi samathehi sammati.

[BJT Page 382]

1. Vivādādhikaraṇaɱ sattannaɱ samathānaɱ dve samathe bhajati. Dve samathe upanissitaɱ dve samathe pariyāpannaɱ dvīhi samathehi saŋgahītaɱ. Dvīhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca.

2. Anuvādādhikaraṇaɱ sattannaɱ samathānaɱ cattāro samathe bhajati. Cattāro samathe upanissitaɱ cattāro samathe pariyāpannaɱ catūhi samathehi saŋgahītaɱ. Catūhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyyasikāya ca.

3. Āpattādhikaraṇaɱ sattannaɱ samathānaɱ tayo samathe bhajati. Tayo samathe upanissitaɱ tayo samathe pariyāpannaɱ tīhi samathehi saŋgahītaɱ. Tīhi samathehi sammati: sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena [page 113] ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.
4. Kiccādhikaraṇaɱ sattannaɱ samathānaɱ ekaɱ samathaɱ bhajati. Ekaɱ samathaɱ upanissitaɱ ekaɱ samathaɱ pariyāpannaɱ ekena samathena saŋgahītaɱ. Ekena samathena sammati: sammukhāvinayenāti.

Bhajativāro niṭṭhito ekavisatimo.

Samathabhedo niṭṭhito

Tassuddānaɱ:
Adhikaraṇaɱ pariyāyaɱ - sādhāraṇā ca bhāgiyā,
Samathā sādhāraṇikā - samathassa tabbhāgiyā.

Samathā sammukhā ceva - vinayena kusalena ca.
Yattha samathā saɱsaṭṭhā - sammati na sammati ca.
Samathādhikaraṇañceva - samuṭṭhānaɱ bhajanti cāti.

Ekuttarikaɱ

Ekakaɱ

1. Āpattikarā dhammā jānitabbā, anāpattikarā dhammā jānitabbā.

Āpatti jānitabbā, anāpatti jānitabbā.

Lahukā āpatti jānitabbā, garukā āpatti jānitabbā.

Sāvasesā āpatti jānitabbā, anavasesā āpatti jānitabbā.

Duṭṭhullā āpatti jānitabbā, aduṭṭhullā āpatti jānitabbā.

Sappaṭikammā āpatti jānitabbā, appaṭikammā āpatti jānitabbā.

Desanāgāminī āpatti jānitabbā, adesanāgāminī āpatti jānitabbā.

Antarāyikā āpatti jānitabbā, anantarāyikā āpatti jānitabbā.

Sāvajjapaññatti āpatti jānitabbā, anavajjapaññatti āpatti jānitabbā.

Kiriyato samuṭṭhitā āpatti jānitabbā, akiriyato samuṭṭhitā āpatti jānitabbā. Kiriyākiriyato samuṭṭhitā āpatti jānitabbā.

Pubbāpatti jānitabbā, aparāpatti jānitabbā.

Pubbāpattīnaɱ antarāpatti jānitabbā, aparāpattīnaɱ antarāpatti jānitabbā.

Desitā gaṇanūpagā āpatti jānitabbā, desitā na gaṇanūpagā āpatti jānitabbā.

Paññatti jānitabbā, anupaññatti jānitabbā. Anuppanna paññatti jānitabbā.

Sabbattha paññatti jānitabbā, padesapaññatti jānitabbā,

Sādhāraṇapaññatti jānitabbā, asādhāraṇapaññatti jānitabbā.

Ekato paññatti jānitabbā, ubhato paññatti jānitabbā.

Thullavajjā āpatti jānitabbā, athullavajjā āpatti jānitabbā.

[BJT Page 010]

Gihīpaṭisaññuttā āpatti jānitabbā, na gihīpaṭisaññuttā āpatti jānitabbā.

Niyatā āpatti jānitabbā, aniyatā āpatti jānitabbā.

Ādikaro puggalo jānitabbo, anādikaro puggalo jānitabbo.

Adhiccāpattiko puggalo jānitabbo, abhiṇhāpattiko puggalo jānitabbo.

Codako puggalo jānitabbo, cuditako puggalo jānitabbo.

Adhammacodako puggalo jānitabbo, adhammacuditako puggalo jānitabbo.

Dhammacodako puggalo jānitabbo, dhammacuditako puggalo jānitabbo.

Niyato puggalo jānitabbo, aniyato puggalo jānitabbo.

Bhabbāpattiko puggalo jānitabbo, abhabbāpattiko puggalo jānitabbo.

Ukkhittako puggalo jānitabbo, anukkhittako puggalo jānitabbo.

Nāsitako puggalo jānitabbo, anāsitako puggalo jānitabbo.

Samānasaɱvāsako puggalo jānitabbo, asamānasaɱvāsako puggalo jānitabbo.
Ṭhapanaɱ jānitabbanti.

Ekakaɱ niṭṭhitaɱ.

Tassuddānaɱ:

1. Karā āpatti lahukā sāvasesā ca duṭṭhullā,
Paṭikammadesanā ceva antarāvajjakiriyā1

2. Kiriyākiriyaɱ pubbā antarā gaṇanūpagā,
Paññatti anānuppanna sabbattha padesasādhāraṇā ca ekato. 2
[page 116]
3. Thullagihīniyatā ca ādi adhicca codakā,
Adhammadhamma niyato abhabbokkhitta nāsitā,
Samānaɱ ṭhapanaɱ ceva uddānaɱ ekake idanti.

1. Paṭikamma desanā ca antarāvajjakiriyaɱ - machasaɱ.
2. Sabbatthādhāranā ca ekako - machasaɱ.
Paññattānuppannā sabbā sādhāraṇe ca ekato - syā.
